# Emberford Marketwalk Microcontent Pack — Emberwild_DepthPack_GIGA_Part2_2025-12-24_MicroPOIs

600 micro-POIs designed to increase moment-to-moment density.

### Emberford Micro-POI 001: Tidehook Turn
- **Vibe:** smells like wet rope and cold iron
- **Gameplay:** 1–2 pulls, a reason to stop, and a reason to leave.
- **Gather / Loot:**
- **Node:** Sun-bleached Coat (ID 43606) — Gear Helm.
- **Node:** Greatwood Biscuit (ID 44817) — Ingredient Fruit.
- **Node:** Harbor-wet Token (ID 40097) — Material Timber.
- **Enemy Packs:**
  - Tide Reavers (dash, knockback)
  - Bogleeches (slow, stacking debuff)
- **Quest Hooks:**
  - Recover a dropped ledger page before dawn.
  - Light three lanterns without being seen.
- **In-World Drop:** a small readable that hints at the area.
- **Design Note:** add one interactable (rope, bell, cache, chalk mark).

### Emberford Micro-POI 002: Lanternpost Hollow
- **Vibe:** too quiet for the time of day
- **Gameplay:** 1–2 pulls, a reason to stop, and a reason to leave.
- **Gather / Loot:**
- **Node:** Frostworn Pendant (ID 41398) — Consumable Potion.
- **Node:** Warden's Trophy Fang (ID 40354) — Ingredient Fish.
- **Node:** Tide-taken Totem (ID 42949) — Consumable Tonic.
- **Enemy Packs:**
  - Rime Crows (blind, peck)
  - Dock Rats (bleed, swarm)
- **Quest Hooks:**
  - Hunt the pack-leader and return a token.
  - Recover a dropped ledger page before dawn.
- **In-World Drop:** a small readable that hints at the area.
- **Design Note:** add one interactable (rope, bell, cache, chalk mark).

### Emberford Micro-POI 003: Rime-Needle Spur
- **Vibe:** warmth where there shouldn't be any
- **Gameplay:** 1–2 pulls, a reason to stop, and a reason to leave.
- **Gather / Loot:**
- **Node:** Pilgrim's Compass (ID 40430) — Gear Dagger.
- **Node:** Storm-bit Coat (ID 43075) — Gear Ring.
- **Node:** Briarbound Plank (ID 42226) — Ingredient Meat.
- **Enemy Packs:**
  - Tide Reavers (dash, knockback)
  - Rime Crows (blind, peck)
- **Quest Hooks:**
  - Mark the safe route with chalk symbols.
  - Follow the cant marks to a hidden cache.
- **In-World Drop:** a small readable that hints at the area.
- **Design Note:** add one interactable (rope, bell, cache, chalk mark).

### Emberford Micro-POI 004: Chalkgate Alcove

- **Node:** Hollowroot Tincture (ID 41548) — Ingredient Salt.

  - Wayward Bandits (nets, call reinforcements)
  - Dock Rats (bleed, swarm)

  - Follow the cant marks to a hidden cache.
